tu phul:_rgyal pos dkon mchog drung du 'bul ba la:_sangs rgyas 'od dpag

gter chen u rgyan gling pas gter nas bton/

pad+ma bka' thang /
la gshegs:_de yi gshegs yul nub phyogs u rgyan yul:_yul gling nyi shu rtsa

gter chen u rgyan gling pas gter nas bton/
dpyid zla ra ba'i rgyal gyi nyin:_bu re skyes te skad kyang mnyam por bton:_ltas

dang bcas:_rgyu ni rin chen dngul las byas pa yi:_dril bu g.yer kha'i dra ba

rigs ldan bde ba bzang skyong zhes bya ba:_phyag rdor sprul pa snang ba'i gzugs 
su grub:_reg pa'i gzugs su ma grub 'od kyi lus_gcer bu skra grol dar sngon 
smad la dkris:_g.yas pa'i phyag na gser gyi rdo rje bsnams:_g.yon pa'i phyag 
na dngul gyi dril bu 'khrol:_'ja' yi rnam pa lta bur bzhugs pa la:_rdzogs pa 
a nu yo ga'i rgyud sde ni:_gsang sngags bla med don rdzogs 'dus pa'i rgyud:_spyi 
rgyud dgu dang sgos rgyud bco lnga gsan:_bye brag rgyud ni brgya phrag bcu rnams 
dang :_gsang chen sgyu 'phrul chen po sde brgyad gsan:_rdor sems sgyu 'phrul 
gsang ba'i snying po dang :_rol pa mngon rdzogs lha mo sgyu 'phrul dang :_dkyil 
'khor rdzogs pa sgyu 'phrul brgyad pa dang :_'phrin las rdzogs pa sgyu 'phrul 
bzhi bcu pa:_ye shes rang snang sgyu 'phrul bla ma dang :_yon tan mthar phyin sgyu 
'phrul brgyad cu pa:_dam tshig mchog tu ston pa le lag dang :_sde snod yongs 
khyab sgyu 'phrul dra ba zhus:_yul gyi ming ni li yi yul du phyin:_dur khrod chen 
po [(]72na[)]lo ka brtsegs zhes pa:_mtha' skor dpag tshad phyed dang bzhi yod 
pa'i:_dbus na rang byung mchod rten ge'u sha:_ma mo chen mo glu sha nI gnas 
pa:_nub byang ljon pa'i dur shing lta na sdug:_dug sbrul 'khril zhing dur phag 
mang pos bskor:_dur bya'i tshang bcas phru gu sha yis gso:_byang shar dur chu dri 
bral mtsho zhes paraH_dur chu'i sems can mang pos sems can za:_la la keng 
rus la la shi la khad:_la la rnyid pa la la phyed tshal dang :_la la gson po mgo 
mjug zar yod pa:_grul bum bu mo ser mo mang po ni:_dur chu'i sems can 
shi tshad pags pa bshu:_shar lhor dur me grib can zhes bya'i gseb:_phag pa 
dkar nag mang po keng rus skyug:_lho nub dur rlung 'tshub 'tshub ces bya'i 
nang :_stag gzig ma bu mang po 'dzing bzhin 'bros:_nub byang dur ri'i rgyal

po srid pa can:_srin bu me khyer mang po me stag 'phro:_dur gyi sems can mang 
po la la shI:_la la na zhing la la 'chi 'phras byed:_la la keng rus la la mda' 
phog pa:_la la gson cing la la lang tsho ldan:_'dod yon 'byung ba nor bu'i 
gter yod pa:_lho na ba lang zhes bya glang po'i gdong :_nag po lus la gzig 
gi thul ba gyon:_lag pa gnyis kyis thod pa'i mdung ring 'dzin:_rgyab na chu 
srin nya yi se le khur:_phag dkar mi ro'i sga cha byas pa zhon:_nub na glang zhon 
nag mo dmar lcam ma:_tri shul rtse gsum thod khrag mi snying za:_shin tu 'jigs 
pa'i dur khrod chen po der:_lo lnga [(]72ba[)]bzhugs nas mkha' 'gror chos 'khor

brtsegs par bzhugs pa'i le'u ste so gsum pa'o:_thatha'abyabya_::
le'u so bzhi pa/_dur khrod chen po gsang chen rol bar bzhugs pa/
!_de nas mkha' spyod rig 'dzin gnas su phyin:_bde chen gsang lam 
mnol ma'i dur khrod na:_mkha' 'gro nyi zla dngos grub ces kyang bya:_mkha' 
'gro'i gtso mo gsang ba ye shes zhes:_dge slong kun dga' smon lam zhes kyang 
bya:_mkha' 'gro las kyi dbang mo che'i drung phyin:_thod mkhar sgo bcad nang du 
ma thar nas:_g.yog mo ku mA ra la 'phrin brgyud pas:_lan ni ma byung brjed 
dam smras pa yis:_shel gyi bum pa khur nas chu len 'dug_ngas bskur byas 
pas bum stegs kha ru bzhag:_rgyal bas bum stegs bum pa 'byar du bcug
longs par ma gyur khug khug lan 'ga' byas:_bum thag phud nas rgyal ba'i 
mdun du 'ongs:_shel gyi gri gus brang bshags kha phye nas:_zhi ba rdo rje dbyings 
kyi lha tshogs rnams:_bkra lam bstan nas ngag nas 'di skad gsungs:_khyod

kyang sngags pa nus mthu can 'dug ste:_de bas nga'i 'di ya mtshan mi che'am:
de skad zer bas phyag btsal bskor ba byas:_mchog dbang gong ma bdag 
la bskur tu gsol:_nga ni g.yog yin nang du 'dengs zer phyin:_nyi zla'i khri 
brtsegs nyi zla'i gdugs phub pa:_nyi ma zla ba'i rgyan drug sku la gsol:_dge 
slong ma bzhugs phyag [(]73na[)]btsal bskor ba byas:_gser gyi 'khor lo rtsibs 
stong phul nas ni:_phyi nang gsang ba'i dbang bskur zhu gsol bas:_lha tshogs 
mdun gyi nam mkhar khra chem byung :_skal ldan rigs ldan da lta dbang zhus 
gsung :_bla ma med pa'i gong rol na:_sangs rgyas bya ba'i ming yang med:
bskal pa stong gi sangs rgyas kyang :_bla ma dag la brten nas byung :_dpal 
ldan bla ma yon tan mtsho:_bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor legs bstan nas:_thugs 
rjes slob ma la gzigs zhu:_dbang ni lha la mi zhu bla mar zhu:_de skad smras pas 
dge slong ma'i zhal nas:_dbang zhu zhes gsung lha tshogs thugs kar bsdus:
rdo rje gro lod yi ge hU~M du bsgyur:_zhal du mid nas byin gyis brlabs pa yis:
phyi ltar sangs rgyas snang ba mtha' yas sku:_tshe yi rigs 'dzin 'grub pa'i 
dbang rnams thob:_khong pa'i nang sleb byin gyis brlabs pa yis:_nang ltar 
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sku:_phyag rgya chen po bsgom pa'i dbang rnams 
thob:_gsang ba'i pad+mor bton nas byin brlabs pas:_lus ngag yid gsum 
shes sgrib dag par sbyangs:_gsang ba ltar na rta mgrin dbang gi sku:_dregs 
pa'i lha 'dre dam la 'dogs dbang thob:_de nas 'og min chos dbyings pho 
brang du:_stug po bkod pa bkod pa lhun grub na:_rgyal ba rgya mtsho rnams kyi 
bka' sdod pa:_rigs 'dzin rdo rje chos ni zhes kyang bya:_rdo rje snying po 'dzin 
pa zhes kyang bya:_rigs 'dzin rgyal po kun dza ra zhes pa:_dung [(]73ba[)]la pho tshos 
bskus pa'i zhal bstan nas:_lha yi bu dang bu mo mang pos bskor:_'ja' dang

'od dang rol mo'i sgra dang bcas:_gnas de nyid du bka' gtad dbang

pad+ma bka' thang /
pa'i dur shing gser ldan la:_dur gyi sems can mang po shing tog len:_nub 
byang dur chu mchog mtsho zhes bya ba:_dur gyi sems can mang po gnas pa yod:
klu dbang gnod sbyin bu mo ro len ma:_byang shar dur ma dud sprin zhes bya ba:
me rlung 'tshub gseb 'dre srin pho mo rnams:_la la mi ro rta ro ba lang dang :
sems can rigs byed za ba dpag med rtse:_shar lhor dur rlung langs 'byin 
zhes bya ba:_kham nag gseb na sems can mi 'dra ba:_dpag tu med pa la la 
shi bar gyur:_la la skye zhing la la rgas pa yod:_nub na dur ri lha min 'bab 
ces par:_dur gyi sems can mang po mi 'dra gnas:_dbul bral yid bzhin 
nor bu'i gter yod pa:_byang na 'du 'chang ma zhes lha mo'i gzugs:_ser mo 
lus la rgod kyi thul ba gyon:_lag pas bam gyi khog stod khog smad 'dral:_rgyab 
na mi mgo rlon pa'i se le khur:_lug nag keng rus sga cha byas pa zhon:_shar na 
ka ca'i bdag mo zhes bya ba:_dmar mo mi ro zhon nas zhing dbyug 'phyar:_shin 
tu 'jigs pa'i dur khrod chen po der:_mchod rten rgyab brten lo lnga'i bar du 
ni:_mkha' [(]74 [)]'gro rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor:_gsang ba'i mtshan ni 
thod 'phreng rtsal du grags:_u rgyan gu ru pad+ma 'byung gnas kyi skyes rabs rnam 
par thar pa rgyas par bkod pa las:_dur khrod chen po gsang chen rol par 
bzhugs pa'i le'u ste so bzhi pa'o:_thathanyargya rgya:

gter chen u rgyan gling pas gter nas bton/

pad+ma bka' thang /
su drang :_nga yis ngan song gsum gyi sgo bcad gsungasaH_sems can bsam 
blo mi gcig tha dad pas:_rang nyid mno ba bzhin du gzhan mi mno:_mi lus 
las ngan kha drag po rnams kun:_nyon mongs nang khang khong khro'i rang bzhin 
tsho:_rnam rtog 'phro 'gyur mang zhing kha lag rtsub:_dmu rgod bsam pa las su 
ma rung rnams:_chos spong la sogs bstan pa'i sel byed pas:_de dag bsgral 
phyir mthu dang ngan sngags dgos:_de phyir ngan sngags chos shig btsal dgos 
bsam:_'jig rten zhing khams dur khrod chen po'i gling :_yul phyogs [(]78na[)]
phung lung nag po'i dur khrod phyin:_mu stegs kha la me 'bar sgo drung du:_'tshub 
ma nag po zhig gi dkyil nang na:_me dmar bya pho tsam zhig ma shi bar:_'jig 
rten dregs pa pho mo thams cad bskor:_sod cig rdungs shig chod cig khrid 
la shog:_sngags pas brjod pa tsham gyis las byed de:_zas su dmar gtor za

bshams pa'i mdun rol du:_lha mi'i sprin phung 'khrigs pa'i dkyil dbus na:

'joms shing bde skyid rdzogs ldan gyi dpal la 'gran pa'i dga' ston la 
spyod pa'i bsams don ma lus pa lhun gyis grub par gyur cig_/mang+galaM//_//
